//
// rook unlock info
//

// - declare property names and flags - all must be listed here
property_decls {
	property		AirmechHPBonusPct							// airmech HP percent bonus amount
	property		AirmechHPBonus					/leadingNum		// flat airmech HP bonus amount
	property		DPSBonus						/leadingNum		// flat airmech DPS bonus (not percent)
	property		DamageBonus									// percentage damage bonus
	property		MeleeDamageBonus							// percentage melee damage bonus (bomber and striker airmech abilities)
	property		MeleeDamage						/leadingNum		// flat melee damage bonus
	property 		MeleeWeaponBonus				/leadingNum	// flag weapon/armor piercing bonus to all melee attacks
	property		GunsDamageBonus								// percentage guns damage bonus
	property		GunsDamage						/leadingNum	// flat guns damage bonus - to all basic guns, but not the sniper rifle
	property 		GunsWeaponBonus					/leadingNum // flag weapon/armor piercing bonus to all guns - guns and ammo type stat
	property		GunsAirDamageBonus							// percentage increase for air guns - multiplicative with 'GunsDamageBonus'
	property		GunsGndDamageBonus							// percentage increase for ground guns - multiplicative with 'GunsDamageBonus'
	property		FuelUseWhenFiringBonus						// percentage *decrease* for air&ground guns energy use when firing: 'FuelUseWhenFiringGnd' and 'FuelUseWhenFiringAir'
	property		SniperDamageBonus							// percentage sniper rifle damage bonus (guns doesn't apply to the sniper rifle)
	property		SniperDamage					/leadingNum	// flat damage bonus to the angel's sniper rifle
	property 		SniperWeapon					/leadingNum	// flat weapon value addition to the angel's sniper rifle
	property 		SniperEnergyEff								// percent *increase* in energy efficiency (per shot) of angel sniper rifle.  +100% = 1/2 energy, +200% = 1/3 energy, etc
	property 		SniperFireRate								// percent *increase* in sniper rifle fire rate - stack's w/ quick shot boost
	property 		SniperRange									// percent *increase* in sniper rifle range - stack's w/ 'AbilitySniperRngScalars' ability level
	property		SniperDeploySpeed							// percent *increase* in sniper deploy speed - modifies 'AbilitySniperModeSpdScalars'
	property		SniperStasisCooldown						// speed *increase* to angel sniper stasis cooldown time (reduces it - efficiency factor multiplier - +100% = 1/2 time, +200% = 1/3 time, etc)
	property		SniperStasisAOERange						// percent *increase* in the sniper statis aoe effect, defined by the radius parameter of the SnoperStasisAOE projectile effect
	property		SniperStasisEnergyEfficiency				// percent *increase* in sniper stasis energy efficiency. Efficiency factor multiplier - +100% = 1/2 energy, +200% = 1/3 energy, etc
	property		KudosBonus									// percentage Kudos bonus
	property		ExperienceBonus								// persistent xp bonus (percentage)
	property		NPLevelXPBonus								// non-persistent level up XP bonus (percentage)
	property		FlightEnergyEfficiencyBonus					// percent *reduction* in energy use, for the purpose of moving only (in air, and on carry cost)
	property		CarryEnergyEfficiencyBonus					// percent *reduction* in energy use, (on carry cost only)
	property		EnergyCapacityBonus							// percent *increase* in energy capacity (actually scales down all consumption)
	property		DamageReduceBonus							// percent *reduction* to damage taken (+100% = 1/2 damage formula)
	property 		DamageEliminationBonus						// percent damage elimination
	property		AirSpeedBonus								// percent speed bonus for air rook movement
	property		GroundSpeedBonus							// percent speed bonus for ground rook movement
	property		TransformSpeedBonus							// percent speed bonus for transforming to/from airmech modes
	property		StartingCreditsBonus						// percent increase/decrease to starting credits amount
	property		CreditsBonus								// percent increase of in-game production credits generation
	property		CreditsCapBonus								// percent increase of in-game production credits CAP
	property		BuildSpeedBonus								// percent *reduction* of unit build times (computed as a reduction in build time, based on an imagined increase in delta time steps)
	property		RespawnTimeBonus							// percent *reduction* to rook respawn/reform time
	property		RechargeRateBonus							// percent increase of rook in-game recharge rate (energy/shields)
	property		RechargeEfficiencyBonus						// percent *reduction* to outpost/fortress power drawn when recharging
	property		StationaryRegenBonus						// percent increase in the stationary/no firing recharge rate of the airmech (FuelRegenOnGroundNoMoveOrFire)
	property		AutoRepairRateBonus							// percent increase of rook's auto repair speed, as well as the activated repair mode
	property		MissileShootDownBonus						// percent chance increase for shooting down missiles
	property		UnitsDamageReduceBonus						// percent *reduction* to all team units damage taken (+100% = 1/2 damage formula)
	property		UnitsAbductResBonus							// percent abduction resistance to all team units
	property		UnitsFireSpeedBonus							// percent speed bonus for all team units firing speed
	property		UnitsDamageBonus							// percent increase for all team units damage done
	property		UnitsArmorBonus				/leadingNum		// flat *increase* to all team units armor value (ArmorType).
	property		UnitsWeaponBonus			/leadingNum		// flat *increase* to all team units weapon value (WeaponType).
	property		UnitsRepairBonus							// percent increase for all team units repair rate
	property		UnitsCarryMassBonus							// percent *reduction* of units carry mass/weight/hp by an airmech
	property		ArmyCommandPointBonus						// percent increase for army command points (unit cap)
	property		ArmyCommandPoints				/leadingNum	// flat increase for army command points (unit cap)
	property		PowerGenBonus
	property		HardCore									// are you hardcore?
	property		DeepBuildQueue					/noDisp				// can you build past the first entry in the queue?
	property		MaxBuildQueue					/trailingNum		// max build orders - 32 is the default in AirMech Command (VR), 14 in other skus
	property		TeamRadarRangeBonus							// percent increase to all team radar ranges
	property		GuardiansFireSpeedBonus						// percent speed bonus for all guardians firing speed
	property		AbilityPointsStartBonus 		/leadingNum		// bonus starting ability points (useful for debugging)
	property 		AllUnitsAttackPowerMod						// percent bonus to all units damage done
	property		InfantrySpeedMod 							// movement speed
	property		InfantryAttackPowerMod 						// damage done to other units
	property		InfantryDamageResistance 					// reduce the damage taken
	property		TankSpeedMod 								// movement speed
	property		TankAttackPowerMod 							// damage done to other units
	property		TankDamageResistance 						// reduce the damage taken
	property		TurretDeploySpeedMod 						// time to get ready after being dropped
	property		TurretAttackPowerMod 						// damage done to other units
	property		TurretDamageResistance 						// reduce the damage taken
	property		MissileSpeedMod 							// applies to player launched missiles and rockets - % increase
	property		MissileDamageMod 							// applies to player launched missiles and rockets - % increase
	property		MissileDamageModAbs				/leadingNum	// applies to player launched missiles and rockets - flat/absolute damage increase value
	property		MissileEnergyEffHelix						// helix missile energy use efficiency; + good (less energy used)
	property		MissileFireRateModHelix						// helix missile fire rate modifier
	property		MissileBurstCooldown						// speed increase to helix/striker  missile missile burst cooldown
	property		MissileBurstAddlSalvos			/leadingNum			// additional missile burst salvos count
	property		MissileBurstAddlMissilePerSalvo /leadingNum			// additional missiles per salvo of the missile burst ability
	property		MissilesWeapon					/leadingNum			// missiles armor piercing/weapon value - for missiles/rockets/grenades (multi-launcher projectiles + missile burst ability)
	property 		MissileModel								// model used for missiles
	property		GunsExplRoundDmg				/leadingNum			// additional blast damage effect on AirMech Ammunition (air and ground)
	property		GunsStasisRoundCh							// chance to stasis effect on AirMech Ammunition (air and ground)
	property		UnitReloadMod 								// time to reload weapon
	property		UnitAimTurnRateMod 							// modifies AimTurnRate
	property		SocketHealRateMod 							// modify heal rate of socketed units (turrets)
	property		YummyCake									// is yummy cake?
	property		MantisStrikeDmgBonus						// percent increase to Mantis Strike damage
	property		MantisStrikeDamage				/leadingNum	// flat damage increase to Mantis Strike projectile
	property		MantisStrikeRngBonus						// percent increase to Mantis Strike range (lifespan)
	property		MantisStrikeWeapon				/leadingNum // flat weapon value addition to the Bomber Mantis Strike attack (armor piercing)
	property		HammerThrowDmgBonus							// percent increase to Hammer Throw damage
	property		HammerThrowDmg					/leadingNum // flag damage increase to Hammer Throw damage
	property 		HammerThrowWeapon				/leadingNum	// flat weapon value addition to the paladin's hammer throw projectile
	property		HammerThrowRngBonus							// percent increase to Hammer Throw range (lifespan)
	property		HammerChargeSpeedBonus						// percent increase to Hammer Charge Speed - and throw speed to match
	property		HammerThrowEnergyEfficiency					// percent *increase* in paladin hammer throw energy efficiency. Efficiency factor multiplier - +100% = 1/2 energy, +200% = 1/3 energy, etc
	property 		HammerStasisTimeBonus						// percent *increase* in paladin hammer stasis duration
	property		AbductSpeedBonus							// percent increase to Saucer Abduction Speed
	property		HealBeamBonus								// percent increase to heal beam effectiveness (base and pct rates)
	property		HealBeamCooldownSpeedBonus					// percent increase to heal beam effect on target cooldown (AMW property)
	property		AllCooldownSpeedBonus						// percent increase to all our cooldowns time passage (legendary type AMW property)
	property		RespawnCostBonus							// percent *decrease* to respawn credit cost
	property		DeathrayBonus								// percent increase to deathray beam damage effectiveness
	property 		DeathrayDamage					/leadingNum	// flat increase to deathray beam damage DPS
	property		DeathrayWeapon					/leadingNum	// flag increase to deathray weapon - armor piercing - value
	property		DeathrayEnergyBonus							// percent *decrease* to deathray beam energy use
	property        DeathrayWarmupSpeed							// percent *increase* to deathray warm up speed.  Base is rook setting: DeathrayWarmupTime in seconds.
	property 		DeathrayRange 								// percent *increase* to deathray range. Base is rook setting: DeathrayRange
	property		AuraRangeBonus								// percent increase to aura range (paladin)
	property		AuraEnergyBonus								// percent *decrease* to aura energy usage (efficiency bonus) (paladin)
	property		PalyShieldBonus								// percent *increase* to paladin's damage reduction w/ shield on frontal attacks
	property 		EMPStasisWeapon					/leadingNum // flag weapon value (armor piercing) addition to the Neo's EMP Stasis attack
	property		EMPRangeBonus								// percent *increase* to neo EMP/Stasis blast effect radius (default is 4.0 units)
	property 		EMPDamage 						/leadingNum // flat *incease* to EMP/stasis blast damage (default is 10 - minimal damage, as main effect is the statis)
	property		EMPCooldown									// speed *increase* to Neo EMP/stasis blast cooldown time (reduces it - efficiency factor multiplier - +100% = 1/2 time, +200% = 1/3 time, etc)
	property 		EMPEnergyEff								// percent *increase* in energy efficiency of Neo EMP/stasis blast.  +100% = 1/2 energy, +200% = 1/3 energy, etc
	property 		EMPStasisTimeBonus							// percent *increase* in Neo EMP stasis duration
	property		EMPExtraBlasts					/leadingNum // additional stasis blast pulses (legendary prop mod)
	property		RadarDisruptCooldown						// speed *increase* to Neo Radar Disrupt cooldown time (reduces it - efficiency factor multiplier - +100% = 1/2 time, +200% = 1/3 time, etc)
	property		RadarDisruptDuration						// duration *increase* to Neo Radar Disrupt effect time
	property		BlinkBoostBonus								// percent *increase* to saucer blink impulse/boost
	property		BlinkEfficiencyBonus						// percent *decrease* to saucer blink energy use
	property 		BlinkCooldownBonus							// percent *increase* in saucer blink cooldown time - effectively reduces 'BlinkTickCooldown' script value
	property		CloakEfficiencyBonus						// percent *decrease* to neo cloak energy use
	property		DebufRangeBonus								// percent *increase* to debuf ability blast effect radius
	property		DebufCooldownBonus							// percent *decrease* to debuf ability cooldowns
	property		HealNovaRangeBonus
	property		EnergyDrainBonus							// percent *increase* in energy drain effectiveness - for the bomber when doing melee dmg w/ the ability of the same name
	property		PwrDrainBonus								// percent energy drain on melee damage (not bomber specific)
	property		HPDrainBonus								// percent hp drain on melee damage
	property		UnitTPCooldownBonus							// percent *decrease* to unit teleport ability cooldown
	property		UnitTPEnergyBonus							// percent *decrease* to unit teleport energy cost
	property		LvlUpHPBonus								// percent *increase* to level up HP reward
	property		LvlUpFuelBonus								// percent *increase* to level up Fuel/Energy reward
	property		SalvageIncomeBonus							// percent *increase* to all salvage income
	property		WarthogSpinUpSpeedBonus						// percent *increase* to warthog's spin up speed on his main gun
	property		AirMechArmorBonus				/leadingNum		// flat *increase* to Airmech's armor value (ArmorType). ('DamageReduceBonus' is a straight damage multiplier - this modifies armor value (ArmorType) of the airmech)
	property		AirMechWeaponBonus				/leadingNum		// flat *increase* to Airmech's weapon value (WeaponType).
	property		GndSpeedWhenFiringBonus						// percent *increase* to airmech ground movement speed when firing
	property		AirSpeedWhenFiringBonus						// percent *increase* to airmech air movement speed when firing
	property		BombImpactDmgBonus							// percent *increase* to airmech bombing direct impact damage
	property		BombImpactDamage				/leadingNum	// flat *increase* to airmech bombing direct impact damage
	property		BombWeapon						/leadingNum // flat weapon value addition to the Bomber Bombs attack (armor piercing)
	property		BombBlastDmgBonus							// percent *increase* to airmech bombing blast damage
	property		BombBlastDamage					/leadingNum	// flat *increase* to airmech bombing blast damage
	property		BombBlastRngBonus							// percent *increase* to airmech bombing blast radius
	property		BombEnergyEffBonus							// percent *increase* to airmech bombing energy efficiency (reduced fuel consumption when using stealth bombing ability)
	property		AirMechKillXPBonus							// percent *increase* to in game XP awarded on AirMech kills
	property		ResurrectCount					/leadingNum // Number of times the mech isn't destroyed after the pre-destroy time ends
	property        BoostRecoveryReduction						// Reduction % in time between boosts
	property        BoostEnergyReduction						// Reduction % in energy cost for boosts
	property		BoostForceBonus								// percent *increase* to boost forceMult
	property		JumpHeightBonus								// percent *increase* to the jump height

	property		UltimateLvl						/trailingNum
	property		UnitBuildLvlReqMod				/trailingNum

	property		DevBits 						/noDisp

	//ability point stats
	property		ABPointSword				/leadingNum		// points to 'sword' ability (on Striker)
	property		ABPointBuilder				/leadingNum		// points to 'builder' ability (on Striker & Helix)
	property		ABPointAfterburner			/leadingNum
	property		ABPointMissileBurst			/leadingNum
	property		ABPointMissiles				/leadingNum
	property		ABPointLifter				/leadingNum

#include unlocks/diamondbundles.txt

rcmd {
	// console run cmd block - 'OnInspectOrUnlock' supports symbol @@ replacement
	// setup common settings for AirMech Heads here
	sym set _CommonHeadCfg_ /scale 4.0 /rotSpeed 30 /pos 3.5 0 1 /scaleMult 1.0
}

/// Colors ////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

// colors - comment out 'hideIfUnlocked' entries so you can always see what you own - kjk

unlockType Blue0 {
	// - 'ColorNone'
	colorName		Blue // map no color to blue. Doesn't count for voting
	category		Color
	noRebuy
	searchTerm		"colors"
	path			menus/IconColor
	tags			showFrame
	descSymbol		ColorNoneDesc
	dispSymbol		ColorNoneDisp
	collectionIgnore
}

unlockType Blue {
	commonName		"Blue Lvl 1"
	category 		Color
	noRebuy
	writeHasSym
	searchTerm		"colors"
	path			menus/IconColor
	tags			showFrame
	onExec			"menuCmd ColorCustomizeCleanup"
	descSymbol		MF_CustomTip_ColorBlue
	dispSymbol		DispColorBlue
}

/// Pilots ////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

unlockType NoPilot {
	category		Pilot
	path			pilots/
	descSymbol		MF_CustomDesc_PilotNoPilot
	dispSymbol		DispPilotNoPilot
	notSelectable
	platformUnlock	dev
	tags			noWishList
	collectionIgnore

	property		DeepBuildQueue					1				// can you build past the first entry in the queue?
	#if airmech_command
		property		MaxBuildQueue					32		// max build orders - 32 is the default in AirMech Command (VR)
	#else
		property		MaxBuildQueue					14		// max build orders - 14 is the default.  MAX is also 14 (ui setup requirement)
	#endif
}

unlockType Junior {
	commonName		"Junior"
	//autoTag			cased
	category		Pilot
	path			pilots/
	descSymbol		MF_CustomDesc_PilotJunior
	dispSymbol		DispPilotJunior
	plevelreq		1	// this is a starter selection pilot

	dynDisp			PMod_Hawk
	property		CreditsCapBonus			100
	property		SalvageIncomeBonus			400

	property		DamageBonus				100
	property		UnitsDamageReduceBonus	50
	property		DamageReduceBonus	100

	property		BuildSpeedBonus			-10			// make easy AI slower to build
	property		AirSpeedBonus			-10			// percent speed bonus for air rook movement
	property		GroundSpeedBonus		-10
	property		TransformSpeedBonus		-2			// percent speed bonus for transforming to/from airmech modes
	property		NPLevelXPBonus			-3			// slower to level up in game
}

	dispSymbol		DispAirMechFighterA
	dynDisp			AMod_FighterA
	uiIndex			0
	customCoords	"650 132 350 186"   "50 0 350 186"
	repairCostBasis 10 // this is the default - kudos/%
	durabilityPerDeath 25 // this is the default
	intrinsic_Power 			450		// 50, 200, 350, 500, 650
	intrinsic_Survivability		450
	intrinsic_Mobility			420
	intrinsic_Army				360
	intrinsic_Special			380
}
